input_tokens) from a context-length 400.\"\"\"\n    m = _CONTEXT_LENGTH_RE.search(error_msg)\n    if m:\n        return int(m.group(1)), int(m.group(2)), int(m.group(3))\n    return None\n\n\ndef _maybe_reduce_max_tokens(oai_request: dict, error_msg: str) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"If the error is a context-length overflow, reduce max_tokens to fit. Returns True if adjusted.\"\"\"\n    parsed = _parse_context_length_error(error_msg)\n    if not parsed:\n        return False\n    ctx_limit, _req_output, input_tokens = parsed\n    headroom = ctx_limit - input_tokens\n    if headroom < 1024:\n        return False\n    new_max = max(1024, headroom - 64)\n    old_max = oai_request.get(\"max_tokens\", 0)\n    if new_max >= old_max:\n        return False\n    oai_request[\"max_tokens\"] = new_max\n    _log(f\"proxy: reduced max_tokens {old_max} -> {new_max} (ctx_limit={ctx_limit}, input={input_tokens})\")\n    return True\n\n\n@_proxy_app.post(\"/v1/messages\")\nasync def _proxy_messages(request: Request):\n    body = await request.json()\n    stream = body.get(\"stream\", False)\n    model = body.get(\"model\", else CHUTES_ROUTING_AGENT\n\n    if stream:\n        last_error_msg = \"\"\n        for attempt in range(1, PROXY_MAX_RETRIES + 1):\n            try:\n                client = generate(resp=resp, cl=client):\n                    try:\n                        _log(f\"proxy: streaming [{routing}] via {routing_label}\")\n                        async for event in Each goal is identified by an integer index and has its own isolated context directory:\n\n```\ncontext/goals/<index>/\n  GOAL.md      — your objective (read-only unless told otherwise)\n  STATE.md     — your working memory and notes to yourself\n  INBOX.md     — messages from the operator (consumed after each step)\n  runs/        — per-step artifacts (rollout.md, logs.txt)\n```\n\nYou are running as **one specific goal**. Your goal index and file paths are shown in the `## Goal` section of your prompt. Only read and write files within your own `context/goals/<index>/` directory.\n\nYour prompt is built from these sources:\n\n- `PROMPT.md` (this file — shared across all goals, do not re-read or edit it)\n- `context/goals/<index>/GOAL.md` (your objective)\n- `context/goals/<index>/STATE.md` (your working memory)\n- `context/goals/<index>/INBOX.md` (operator notes, cleared after each step)\n- Recent Telegram chat history from `context/chat/` (shared operator chat)\n\nThe goal loop only runs while the goal's `GOAL.md` is non-empty and the goal is started.\n\nAfter each step, artifacts are saved to `context/goals/<index>/runs/<timestamp>/`.\n\nEach loop iteration is called a step — a single call to the Claude Code CLI (`claude -p`). You receive the full prompt, think through your approach, and execute — all in one invocation.\n\nSteps run back-to-back with no delay on success. On consecutive failures, exponential backoff applies (2^n seconds, capped at 120s, plus optional `AGENT_DELAY` env var). Each goal can also have its own per-goal delay.\n\nThe operator is a human who communicates with you through Telegram. Their messages are processed by the Claude Code CLI in this repository to perform actions like restarting the pm2 process, pausing goals, adapting the code, updating your goal and state, and relaying your messages. The chat history is stored as rolling JSONL files in `context/chat/`. You can also send messages to the operator (`python arbos.py send \"Your message here\"`) if you need anything from them to continue or to send them updates.\n\nFiles sent by the operator via Telegram are saved to `context/files/` and their path is included in the operator message. Text files under 8 KB are also inlined. To send files back to the operator, use `python arbos.py sendfile path/to/file [--caption 'text']`. Add `--photo` to send images as compressed photos instead of documents.\n\nTo restart the process after self-modifying code, touch the `.restart` flag file (`touch .restart`) and pm2 will restart the process.\n\n## How steps work\n\nYou have **no memory between steps**. Each step is a fresh CLI invocation. The only continuity is what's written to your `STATE.md` — if you don't write it there, your next step won't know about it.\n\nEach step runs with full permissions (`--dangerously-skip-permissions`). Plan your approach at the start of each step, then execute. There is no separate plan phase — think and act in a single pass.\n\nPrevious run artifacts (`context/goals/<index>/runs/*/rollout.md`, etc.) are **not** included in your prompt. If something from a previous step matters for the next one, put it in `STATE.md`.\n\n## Conventions\n\n- **State**: Keep your `STATE.md` short, high-signal, and action-oriented.\n- **Goal**: Do not edit your `GOAL.md` unless the operator explicitly asks for that.\n- **Chat history**: The durable operator interaction log lives in `context/chat/*.jsonl`.\n- **Run artifacts**: Step-specific outputs live in `context/goals/<index>/runs/<timestamp>/`.\n- **Shared tools**: Put reusable scripts in `tools/` when they are generally useful.\n- **Background processes**: Use `pm2` for long-lived processes and leave enough breadcrumbs in `STATE.md` for the next step.\n- **Be proactive**: Work in stages, keep notes for your future self, and keep moving toward the goal.\n\n## Inference\n\nYou get your inference from Chutes (chutes.ai) via the Claude Code CLI. This is the provider powering each step and the operator bot. Target: >=65% accuracy, >90 bets/month, positive Sharpe.\n\n## Current Status: ✅ Step 14 Completed - Next: Step 15 Tighten Confidence & Add Diversity\n\n### Step 14 Results (20260318_080126)\n- **Config:** MIN_CONFIDENCE lowered to 0.65 (from 0.75), MIN_MODELS_AGREE=2, MODEL_TYPES=[\"random_forest\"], RF max_depth=8/min_samples_leaf=10, Horizons: 15m only\n- **Data:** 8641 samples (90 days), 4000 train max, 31 features\n- **Population:** 5 identical RFs (fitness 0.77)\n- **Validation:** Train: 2209, Valid: 672 (single split)\n- **Metrics:**\n  - Accuracy: **0.5517** ❌ (below 65%)\n  - Bets/month: **126.11** ✅ (exceeds 90)\n  - Sharpe: **-27.37** ❌ (deeply negative)\n  - Max drawdown: 0.0199 (1.99%)\n  - Total return: -0.0199 (-1.99%)\n  - Generated 2880 signals, consensus filtered to ~126 bets/month\n  - Latest signal: -1 (NO_TRADE)\n- **Observation:** Lowering confidence threshold drastically increased trade frequency but accuracy collapsed and Sharpe turned highly negative. All models identical, so consensus gate (2/5) is trivial; confidence is the only effective filter.\n\n### Reflection Step 14\n**Why accuracy target missed?** Walk-forward validation accuracy is only 55.2%, barely above random. The model lacks predictive power for 15-minute direction. The fitness during evolution (0.77) appears overfitted to training; out-of-sample performance is poor.\n\n**Why Sharpe negative?** The bets are generating net losses, with a Sharpe of -27.37 indicating severe negative expectancy. Lowering confidence admitted many low-quality signals that lose money on average.\n\n**Consensus gate:** With 5 identical random forest clones, MIN_MODELS_AGREE=2 is automatically satisfied for any non-zero prediction. The gate effectively reduces to MIN_CONFIDENCE alone, which is not a reliable proxy for correctness.\n\n**Model diversity:** Population is not diverse (all same architecture and hyperparams). Evolutionary search explores only a single point, limiting the value of consensus.\n\n**Bet frequency:** Target exceeded (126/month) — successful relaxation.\n\n**Overall diagnosis:** The model's predictive signal is too weak to profitably trade even with moderate confidence threshold. The current confidence-based filtering is insufficient to discriminate winning vs losing trades. We need both tighter confidence selection AND improved model quality/diversity to restore accuracy and profitability.\n\n### Step 15 Plan\n**Objective:** Restore accuracy >65% and Sharpe >0 while keeping bets/month >90.\n**Challenges:** Current 126 bets/month gives headroom to tighten selection by ~20% and still stay above 90.\n\n**Proposed changes:**\n1. **Tighten confidence threshold** to restore precision: raise MIN_CONFIDENCE from 0.65 → **0.70** (or possibly 0.72). This should filter out lower-confidence bets, potentially improving accuracy and Sharpe, while likely keeping >90 bets/month given current headroom.\n2. **Introduce model diversity** to make consensus meaningful: change MODEL_TYPES from [\"random_forest\"] to **[\"random_forest\", \"simple_nn\"]**. This will produce heterogeneous predictions; the consensus gate (MIN_MODELS_AGREE=2) will then require agreement across different model families, which should be a stronger signal.\n3. Keep MIN_MODELS_AGREE=2 (maintain 2-of-5 agreement; with 5 models total population).\n4. Keep HORIZONS={\"15m\":1} for now (avoid complexity until performance stabilizes).\n5. If performance remains poor, consider:\n   - Expanding horizons (1h, 4h) as contextual features\n   - Increasing model capacity (RF max_depth=10, min_samples_leaf=5)\n   - Using more training samples (MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES=6000 or None)\n   - Adjusting fitness to use validation Sharpe directly\n\n**Expected:** Higher confidence + diverse ensemble should yield fewer but higher-quality trades, pushing accuracy back above 65% and Sharpe positive, while staying above 90 bets/month.\n\n### Prior Steps Summary\n- Steps 7-9: Zero bets due to overly strict consensus (3 models @ 0.80, then 2 @ 0.75) and logistic regression interference.\n- Step 10-12: Configuration introspection only (no trading run).\n- Step 13: First run with MIN_CONFIDENCE=0.75, generated 8.7 bets/month (high confidence, tiny sample).\n- Step 14: Lowered confidence to 0.65, achieved 126 bets/month but accuracy dropped to 55% and Sharpe deeply negative. Bet frequency target met, but quality metrics failed.\n\n### Configuration Snapshot (as of Step 14)\n- MODEL_TYPES = [\"random_forest\"]\n- RANDOM_FOREST_N_ESTIMATORS = [50]\n- RANDOM_FOREST_MAX_DEPTH = [8]\n- RANDOM_FOREST_MIN_SAMPLES_LEAF = [10]\n- HORIZONS = {\"15m\": 1}\n- MIN_MODELS_AGREE = 2\n- MIN_CONFIDENCE = 0.65\n\n**Proposed Step 15 changes:**\n- MIN_CONFIDENCE = 0.70\n- MODEL_TYPES = [\"random_forest\", \"simple_nn\"]\n- Keep other hyperparams unchanged for now.\n\n### Next Checkpoint\nAfter Step 15 run, evaluate:\n- Bets/month > 90?\n- Accuracy >= 65%?\n- Sharpe > 0?\nIf any target missed: iterate with further confidence adjustments or model diversity additions."}}],"model":"stepfun/step-3.5-flash:free","stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"output_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":null,"cache_read_input_tokens":null,"cache_creation":null,"inference_geo":null,"server_tool_use":null,"service_tier":null},"provider":"StepFun","context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"833e0393-fe58-4cbf-8eff-f08b5ef0e12b","uuid":"e5fe7554-74c8-4ea6-bf66-5e2b42584c3b"}
